Video Player! is also designed to allow businesses to more effectively share videos of conference keynotes or presentations, allowing users to navigate directly to the segments of the video that interest them. \r\n\r\nVideo Player! also provides an excellent way for law enforcement and security professionals to review video from body cameras or security video.\r\n\r\nVideo Player! provides support for the Surface Dial, allowing users to rotate the dial to advance or rewind the video and to capture frames using the Surface Dial button.\r\n\r\nAn in-app purchase is required to save the captured frames although an in-app purchase is not required to view a frames file created by another user.\r\n\r\nThe video 'Flying Full Circle' is shown in the screenshots with the permission of Terwilliger Productions.
